 ' US military aid accounted for 21 percent of Pakistan's defense spending between 2002 and 2015, helping Pakistan maintain its high levels of military procurement while reducing the burden on its federal budget and the overall economy
 report main kaha gaya he ki pakistan ke saath dwipaksheeya sambandhon ke liye washington main sahyog main kami ai he, kyonki pakistan afghanistan or bharat main dhyaan kendrit karne vaale hinsak ativaadee samoohon sambandhi chintaaon se nipatane main aksham yaa anicchhuk prathit hota he
 The report said that India is a bigger and more attractive market for global defense companies and will remain so in the near future
 bharat hathiyaaron kaa vishwa main sabase bada ayatak ban gaya he
 India imported 14 percent of global weapons from 2011 to 2015, an increase of 90 percent compared to the five years before

 "it says," Pakistan will have to make a difficult choice to buy expensive weapon systems over the long term until it gets these at discounted rates
 ' The report said that Pakistan would have to bear the bulk of its defense purchases due to an 'almost certain decline' in financial and military cooperation from the US
 report main kaha gaya he ki sainya kharidari ke maamle main pakistan bharat ke saath muqabla nahin kar saktaa or isi liye vah parmaanu hathiyaaron main kharch badha saktaa he
